ABSTRACT 

In  this  work  we  intend  to  join  the  objectives  of  both  the  Klein  Workshops  and  the 
Structuring Content - Functions, in the Basic Education Curriculum Guidelines and to 
study  an  article  from  the  Klein  Mathematics  Project  in  Portuguese:  Polynomial 
Functions and the Digital World of Wanderley Moura Rezende responding to several 
questions  raised  by  the  target  audience.  The  objective  of  this  work  is  to  produce  a 
material that provides the reader with an independent analysis that he can get within 
the text itself, heal his doubts in order to properly understand the material studied. 

Key  words:  Trigonometric  functions.  Polynomial  functions.  Exponential  functions. 
Approximation of functions. Taylor polynomial. Paper Klein.
